
-----title
西安 (出生地)

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=831&endYear=831')">831年</a>　退居长安西南原上，村居有诗。作品：《村居即事》<div id='poem_8293' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8293' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_0_8293'>休看小字大书名，向日持经眼却明。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8293'>时过无心求富贵，身闲不梦见公卿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8293'>因寻寺里<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_8293", 8293, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>薰辛</span>断，自别城中礼数生。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8293'>斜月照房新睡觉，西峰半夜鹤来声。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8293'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_8293_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_content_8297'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8297'>老病贪光景，寻常不下帘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8297'>妻愁耽酒僻，人怪考诗严。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8297'>小婢偷红纸，娇儿弄白髯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8297'>有时看旧卷，未免意中嫌。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8297'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_8297_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=831&endYear=831')">831年</a>　退居长安西南原上，有诗赠洪哲师。作品：《赠洪哲师》<div id='poem_8384' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8384' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>中听</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8384'>识病方书圣，谙山草木灵。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8384'>人来多<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作还）</span>施药，愿满不持经。<div /></div>

邢台

id='poem_sentence_4_8418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_8418'>开泉浴山禽，为爱山中声。<div id='poem_sentence_5_8418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_8418'>世间事难保，一日各徂征。<div id='poem_sentence_6_8418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_8418'>死生不相及，花落实方荣。<div id='poem_sentence_7_8418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_8418'>我来至此中，守吏非本名。<div id='poem_sentence_8_8418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_8418'>重君昔为主，相与下马行。<div id='poem_sentence_9_8418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_8418'>旧岛日日摧，池水不复清。<div id='poem_sentence_10_8418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_8418'>岂无后人赏，所贵手自营。<div id='poem_sentence_11_8418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_8418'>浇酒向所思，风起如有灵。<div id='poem_sentence_12_8418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_8418'>此去不重来，重来伤我形。<div id='poem_sentence_13_8418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_8418'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_8418_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
邯郸

id='poem_title_8502_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8502'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8502'>孤贱相长<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作长相）</span>育，未曾为远游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8502'>谁不重欢爱，晨昏阙珍羞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8502'>出门念衣单，草木当穷秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8502'>非疾有忧叹，实为人子尤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8502'>世情本难合，对面隔山丘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_8502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_8502'>况复干戈地，儒夫何所投。<div id='poem_sentence_5_8502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_8502'>与尔俱长成，尚为沟壑忧。<div id='poem_sentence_6_8502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_8502'>岂非轻岁月，少小不勤修。<div id='poem_sentence_7_8502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_8502'>从今解思量，勉力谋善猷。<div id='poem_sentence_8_8502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_8502'>但<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作伊）</span>得成尔身，衣食宁我求。<div id='poem_sentence_9_8502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_8502'>固合受此训，堕<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作惰）</span>慢为身羞<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作雠）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_8502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_8502'>岁暮当归来，慎莫怀远游。<div id='poem_sentence_11_8502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_8502'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_8502_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

大名

class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>出使荆南，抵达江陵，结识荆南节度使赵宗儒、使府掌书记杜元颖和从事李肇。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>出使荆南，游江陵，有诗纪事。作品：《江陵纪事》<div id='poem_8287' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8287' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8287?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江陵即事</a><span class='inlineComment2'>（一作头）</span>压大堤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8287'>蜀女下沙迎水客，巴童傍驿卖山鸡。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8287'>寺多红药烧人眼，地足青苔染马蹄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8287'>夜半独眠愁在远，北看归路隔蛮溪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8287'></div><div id='poem_sentence_0_8485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8485'>素传学道徒<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作素业传学徒）</span>，清门有君子。<div id='poem_title_8501_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8501'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8501'>海人无家海里住，采珠役<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作杀）</span>象为岁赋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8501_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8501'>恶波横天山塞路，未央宫中常满库。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8501_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8501'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_8501_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年</a>　出使岭南，春在广州，观蛮妓，有诗记之。作品：《观蛮妓》<div id='poem_8076' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8076' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_8076'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8076'>欲说昭君敛翠蛾，清声委曲怨于歌。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8076_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8076'>谁家年少春风里，抛与金钱唱好多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8076_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8076'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_8076_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年</a>　出使岭南，春,在广州，有诗乞官东都。作品：《寄分司张郎中》<div id='poem_8503' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8503' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8503?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄分司张郎中</a><span class='authorDate'>（811年）</span><span id='poem_sentence_0_8503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8503'>声名已压众人上，愁思未平双鬓知。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8503'>江郡迁移犹远地，仙官荣宠是分司。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8503'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_8503", 8503, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>青天白日</span>当头上，会有求闲不得时。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8503'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_8503_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
常德
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ee5192ead4fa4f4daf95907ab220035e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ee5192ead4fa4f4daf95907ab220035e");'><span id='ee5192ead4fa4f4daf95907ab220035e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年</a>，46岁</div><div id='ee5192ead4fa4f4daf95907ab220035e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年</a>　出使岭南，春末北返，途经武陵，有诗纪行。作品：《武陵春日》<div id='poem_8305' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8305' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8305?labeling=true' target='_blank'>武陵春日</a><span class='authorDate'>（811年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18501, "中唐", "王建", "poem_title_8305")'>王建</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_8305_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8305'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8305'>寻春何事却悲凉，春到他乡忆故乡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8305'>秦女洞桃欹涧碧，楚王堤柳舞烟黄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8305'>波涛入梦家山远，名利关身客路长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8305'>不似冥心叩尘寂，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_8305", 8305, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>玉编</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_8305", 8305, "Clauses/7/Comments/1")'>金轴</span>有仙方。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8305'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_8305_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
陕西
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f59d9503cba64e12a43206be1a6e0f03_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f59d9503cba64e12a43206be1a6e0f03");'><span id='f59d9503cba64e12a43206be1a6e0f03_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=821&endYear=821')">821年</a>，56岁</div><div id='f59d9503cba64e12a43206be1a6e0f03' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在秘书郎任，妻李氏亡故，请丧假回渭河南岸山庄小住，曾赋诗纪行。作品：《初冬旅行》<div id='poem_8080' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8080' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8080?labeling=true' target='_blank'>初冬旅游</a><span class='authorDate'>（821年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18501, "中唐", "王建", "poem_title_8080")'>王建</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_8080_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8080'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8080'>远投人宿趁房迟，僮仆伤寒马亦饥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8080'>为客悠悠十月尽，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_8080", 8080, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>庄头</span>栽竹已过时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8080'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_8080_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在秘书郎任，冬末，仍居渭河南岸山庄，曾赋诗自伤身世。作品：《自伤》<div id='poem_8288' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8288' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8288?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自伤</a><span class='authorDate'>（821年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18501, "中唐", "王建", "poem_title_8288")'>王建</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_8288_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8288'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8288'>衰门海内几多人，满眼公卿总不亲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8288_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8288'>四授官资元七品，再经婚娶尚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_8288", 8288, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>单身</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8288_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8288'>图书亦为频移尽，兄弟还因数散贫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_8288_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_8288'>独自在家长似客，黄昏哭向野田春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_8288_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_8288'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_8288_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_8288'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(8288)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
三门峡
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2da8b3b734704dd6be7151bf3fbb4b19_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2da8b3b734704dd6be7151bf3fbb4b19");'><span id='2da8b3b734704dd6be7151bf3fbb4b19_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>，64岁</div><div id='2da8b3b734704dd6be7151bf3fbb4b19' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年4月</a>　在陕州司马任，白居易返洛阳赴太子宾客任，路经陕州，王建与陕虢观察使王起相迎宴叙。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　在陕州司马任，有诗寄刘蕡。作品：《寄刘蕡问疾》<div id='poem_8209' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_8209' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/8209?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄刘蕡问疾</a><span class='authorDate'>（829年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18501, "中唐", "王建", "poem_title_8209")'>王建</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_8209_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_8209'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_8209'>年少病多应为酒，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_8209", 8209, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>谁家</span>将息过今春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_8209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_8209'>赊来半夏重熏<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作煎）</span>尽，投著山中旧主人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_8209_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_8209'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_8209_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
